            return "{}"

                for v142 in ListaP:gmatch("Nome%s*=%s*\".-\"\n.-Texto%s*=%s*\".-\"") do
                    local v143 = (v142:match("Nome%s*=%s*\"([^\"]+)\"") or ""):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$");
                    local v144 = (v142:match("CorPrincipal%s*=%s*\"([^\"]+)\"") or "0:0:0"):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$");
                    local v145 = (v142:match("CorDisplay%s*=%s*\"([^\"]+)\"") or "#FFFFFF"):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$");
                    local v146 = (v142:match("CorNome%s*=%s*\"([^\"]+)\"") or "#FFFFFF"):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$");

                    local v150 = (v142:match("Texto%s*=%s*\"([^\"]+)\"") or ""):match("^%s*(.-)%s*$");
                    local v151, v152, v153 = v144:match("(%d+):(%d+):(%d+)");
                    local v154 = v151 or "0";
                    local v155 = v152 or "0";
                    if not v153 then
                        v153 = "0";

                        v143, 
                        tonumber(v154), 
                        tonumber(v155), 
                        tonumber(v153), 
                        v145, 
                        v146, 
                        v147, 
                        v148, 
                        v149, 
                        v150
                    };
                end;

            Protegido = function(v156) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                if table.find(Safelist, v156) then
                    return false;

                    return Config.AtacarDev;
                elseif table.find(Admins, v156) then
                    return Config.AtacarAdmin;

                    return Config.AtacarElite;

                    return Config.AtacarPremium;

                    return true;

            Configurar = function(v190) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                local v191 = true;
                for v192 = 0, 60 do
                    local v193 = _G["Frame" .. v192];
                    if v193 and (v190 ~= "nulo" and v192 == v190) ~= v193.Visible then
                        v191 = false;
                        break;
                    end;
                end;
                if v191 then
                    return;
                else
                    for v194 = 0, 60 do
                        local v195 = _G["Frame" .. v194];
                        if v195 then
                            v195.Visible = v190 ~= "nulo" and v194 == v190;
                        end;
                    end;
                    return;
                end;
            end;

                    v199:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel") and v199.ImageLabel:FindFirstChild("UIStroke")
                }) do
                    if v202 then
                        if v200 then
                            tweens[v202] = criarTween(v202);
                            Som("77120543307812");

                                Configurar("nulo");
                            else
                                Configurar(0);
                            end;
                        else
                            if tweens[v202] then
                                tweens[v202]:Cancel();
                                tweens[v202] = nil;
                            end;
                            v202.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0);
                        end;
                    end;
                end;
            end;

            RejoinBotao.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                if #game.Players:GetPlayers() <= 1 then
                    Notificar("Rejoin", traducao.RejoinText, 5);
                else
                    coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                        local l_TeleportService_0 = game:GetService("TeleportService");
                        local l_Players_0 = game:GetService("Players");
                        local l_status_26, l_result_26 = pcall(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                            -- upvalues: l_TeleportService_0 (ref), l_Players_0 (ref)
                            l_TeleportService_0:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, l_Players_0.LocalPlayer);
                        end);
                        if not l_status_26 then
                            warn(l_result_26);
                        end;
                    end));
                end;
            end);
            ServerHop = function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                PlaceID = PlaceID or game.PlaceId;
                foundAnything = foundAnything or "";
                site = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. PlaceID .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100" .. (foundAnything ~= "" and "&cursor=" .. foundAnything or "")));
                if #site.data == 0 then
                    Notificar("ServerHop", traducao.ShErro, 6);
                    return true;
                else
                    local v254 = nil;
                    maxPlayers = 0;
                    bestServerID = v254;
                    for _, v256 in pairs(site.data) do
                        local v257 = tostring(v256.id);
                        local v258 = tonumber(v256.playing);
                        max = tonumber(v256.maxPlayers);
                        playing = v258;
                        id = v257;
                        if playing < max and id ~= game.JobId and maxPlayers < playing then
                            v257 = id;
                            maxPlayers = playing;
                            bestServerID = v257;
                        end;
                    end;
                    if bestServerID then
                        wait();
                        pcall(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                            wait();
                            game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(PlaceID, bestServerID, game.Players.LocalPlayer);
                        end);
                        return;
                    else
                        Notificar("ServerHop", traducao.ShErro, 6);
                        return true;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
            ServerHopBotao.MouseButton1Click:Connect(ServerHop);
            Ancorar = function(v259) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character then
                    for _, v261 in ipairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v261:IsA("BasePart") then
                            v261.Anchored = v259;
                        end;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
            Freecam = function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                cam = workspace.CurrentCamera;
                UIS = game:GetService("UserInputService");
                RS = game:GetService("RunService");
                onMobile = not UIS.KeyboardEnabled;
                keysDown = {};
                rotating = false;
                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                    game.Loaded:Wait();
                end;
                cam.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable;
                speed = 5;
                sens = 0.4;
                speed = speed / 10;
                if onMobile then
                    sens = sens * 2;
                end;
                renderStepped = function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    if rotating then
                        Ancorar(true);
                        delta = UIS:GetMouseDelta();
                        cf = cam.CFrame;
                        yAngle = cf:ToEulerAngles(Enum.RotationOrder.YZX);
                        newAmount = math.deg(yAngle) + delta.Y;
                        if (newAmount > 65 or newAmount < -65) and (yAngle >= 0 or delta.Y >= 0) and (yAngle <= 0 or delta.Y <= 0) then
                            delta = Vector2.new(delta.X, 0);
                        end;
                        cf = cf * CFrame.Angles(-math.rad(delta.Y), 0, 0);
                        cf = CFrame.Angles(0, -math.rad(delta.X), 0) * (cf - cf.Position) + cf.Position;
                        cf = CFrame.lookAt(cf.Position, cf.Position + cf.LookVector);
                        if delta ~= Vector2.new(0, 0) then
                            cam.CFrame = cam.CFrame:Lerp(cf, sens);
                        end;
                        UIS.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCurrentPosition;
                    else
                        UIS.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default;
                    end;
                    if keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.W"] then
                        cam.CFrame = cam.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 0, -speed));
                    end;
                    if keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.A"] then
                        cam.CFrame = cam.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(-speed, 0, 0));
                    end;
                    if keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.S"] then
                        cam.CFrame = cam.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 0, speed));
                    end;
                    if keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.D"] then
                        cam.CFrame = cam.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(speed, 0, 0));
                    end;
                end;
                renderSteppedConnection = RS.RenderStepped:Connect(renderStepped);
                validKeys = {
                    "Enum.KeyCode.W", 
                    "Enum.KeyCode.A", 
                    "Enum.KeyCode.S", 
                    "Enum.KeyCode.D"
                };
                UIS.InputBegan:Connect(function(v262) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    for _, v264 in pairs(validKeys) do
                        if v264 == tostring(v262.KeyCode) then
                            keysDown[v264] = true;
                        end;
                    end;
                    if v262.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2 or v262.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch and UIS:GetMouseLocation().X > cam.ViewportSize.X / 2 then
                        rotating = true;
                    end;
                    if v262.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch and v262.Position.X < cam.ViewportSize.X / 2 then
                        touchPos = v262.Position;
                    end;
                end);
                UIS.InputEnded:Connect(function(v265) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    for v266, _ in pairs(keysDown) do
                        if v266 == tostring(v265.KeyCode) then
                            keysDown[v266] = false;
                        end;
                    end;
                    if v265.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2 or v265.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch and UIS:GetMouseLocation().X > cam.ViewportSize.X / 2 then
                        rotating = false;
                    end;
                    if v265.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch and touchPos and v265.Position.X < cam.ViewportSize.X / 2 then
                        touchPos = nil;
                        keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.W"] = false;
                        keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.A"] = false;
                        keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.S"] = false;
                        keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.D"] = false;
                    end;
                end);
                UIS.TouchMoved:Connect(function(v268) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    if touchPos and v268.Position.X < cam.ViewportSize.X / 2 then
                        if v268.Position.Y < touchPos.Y then
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.W"] = true;
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.S"] = false;
                        else
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.W"] = false;
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.S"] = true;
                        end;
                        if v268.Position.X < touchPos.X - 15 then
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.A"] = true;
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.D"] = false;
                        elseif v268.Position.X > touchPos.X + 15 then
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.A"] = false;
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.D"] = true;
                        else
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.A"] = false;
                            keysDown["Enum.KeyCode.D"] = false;
                        end;
                    end;
                end);
            end;
            DesligarFC = function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                if renderSteppedConnection then
                    Ancorar(false);
                    renderSteppedConnection:Disconnect();
                end;
                local l_CurrentCamera_0 = workspace.CurrentCamera;

                    wait();

            OrganizarLista = function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                posicaoAtual = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 10);
                listaOrdenada = {};
                for _, v405 in ipairs(MenuPlayers:GetChildren()) do
                    if v405:IsA("ImageButton") and v405.Visible then
                        local v406 = v405.Name:split(":")[2];
                        local v407 = 7;
                        if v406 == game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name then
                            v407 = 0;
                        else
                            for v408, v409 in ipairs({
                                Devs, 
                                Admins, 
                                Elites, 
                                Premiums, 
                                PremiumsTemp, 
                                Usuarios
                            }) do
                                for _, v411 in ipairs(v409) do
                                    if v411 == v406 then
                                        v407 = v408;
                                        break;
                                    end;
                                end;
                                if v407 ~= 7 then
                                    break;
                                end;
                            end;
                        end;
                        table.insert(listaOrdenada, {
                            v405, 
                            v407
                        });
                    end;
                end;
                table.sort(listaOrdenada, function(v412, v413) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    return v412[2] < v413[2];
                end);
                for _, v415 in ipairs(listaOrdenada) do
                    v415[1].Position = posicaoAtual;
                    posicaoAtual = UDim2.new(0, posicaoAtual.X.Offset, 0, posicaoAtual.Y.Offset + 60 + espacoEntre);
                end;
                FIMFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, posicaoAtual.Y.Offset + 3);
            end;

                PesquisarBox.Text = string.gsub(PesquisarBox.Text, " ", "");

                    CancelarBusca();
                    return;
                else
                    AutoAdd = false;
                    encontrou = false;
                    for _, v419 in ipairs(MenuPlayers:GetChildren()) do
                        if v419:IsA("ImageButton") and v419.Name:find(":") then
                            local v420 = string.split(v419.Name, ":");
                            if v420[1]:lower():sub(1, #PesquisarBox.Text) == PesquisarBox.Text:lower() or v420[2]:lower():sub(1, #PesquisarBox.Text) == PesquisarBox.Text:lower() then
                                v419.Visible = true;
                                encontrou = true;
                            else
                                v419.Visible = false;
                            end;
                        end;
                    end;

                        MenuPlayers.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, 0);
                        OrganizarLista();
                    else
                        MenuPlayers.Visible = false;
                        SemResultado.Visible = true;
                        TextoSR.Visible = true;
                        TextoSR.Text = traducao.NoResult .. " '" .. PesquisarBox.Text .. "'";
                    end;

                end;

            Listar = function(v483) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                coroutine.wrap(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    -- upvalues: v483 (ref)

                        -- upvalues: v483 (ref)
                        return game:GetService("Players"):GetUserIdFromNameAsync(v483);
                    end);
                    if not l_status_27 or not l_result_27 then
                        Notificar(traducao.Erro, traducao.ErroObterPlayer, 6);
                        return;
                    else
                        local l_status_28, l_result_28 = pcall(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                            -- upvalues: l_result_27 (ref)
                            return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://users.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. l_result_27));
                        end);
                        if not l_status_28 or not l_result_28 then
                            Notificar(traducao.Erro, traducao.ErroObterPlayer, 6);
                            return;
                        else
                            local v488 = l_result_28.displayName or v483;
                            local l_name_0 = l_result_28.name;
                            if not table.find(Safelist, l_name_0) then
                                table.insert(Safelist, l_name_0);
                            end;
                            pcall(Safe, l_name_0, "add");

            RequerMao = true;
            KillAuraAtiva = false;
            _G.KillAura = function(v854) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                if KillAuraConnection then
                    KillAuraConnection:Disconnect();
                end;
                KillAuraAtiva = v854;
                pcall(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                    -- upvalues: v854 (ref)
                    ConfigFile("KillAura", v854);
                end);
                if not KillAuraAtiva then
                    return;
                else
                    KillAuraConnection = game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                        local l_LocalPlayer_15 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer;
                        local l_Character_9 = l_LocalPlayer_15.Character;
                        local v857 = l_Character_9 and l_Character_9:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
                        if not v857 then
                            return;
                        else
                            if RequerMao then
                                local v858 = false;
                                for _, v860 in ipairs(l_Character_9:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v860:IsA("Tool") and v860:FindFirstChild("DamageRemote") then
                                        v858 = true;
                                        break;
                                    end;
                                end;
                                if not v858 then
                                    return;
                                end;
                            end;
                            local v861 = nil;
                            local v862 = 16;
                            for _, v864 in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if v864 ~= l_LocalPlayer_15 then
                                    local l_Character_10 = v864.Character;
                                    local v866 = l_Character_10 and l_Character_10:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
                                    local v867 = l_Character_10 and l_Character_10:FindFirstChild("ForceField");
                                    local v868 = l_Character_10 and l_Character_10:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
                                    if v866 and v866.Health > 0 and not v867 and v868 and Protegido(v864.Name) then
                                        local v869 = false;
                                        for _, v871 in ipairs(l_Character_10:GetChildren()) do
                                            if v871:IsA("Tool") and v871.Name == "Kawaii Revolver" then
                                                v869 = true;
                                                break;
                                            end;
                                        end;
                                        if not v869 then
                                            local l_Backpack_0 = v864:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack");
                                            if l_Backpack_0 then
                                                for _, v874 in ipairs(l_Backpack_0:GetChildren()) do
                                                    if v874:IsA("Tool") and v874.Name == "Kawaii Revolver" then
                                                        v869 = true;
                                                        break;
                                                    end;
                                                end;
                                            end;
                                        end;
                                        if v869 and (not SomenteAlvos or table.find(Alvos, v864.Name)) then
                                            local l_Magnitude_0 = (v868.Position - v857.Position).Magnitude;
                                            if l_Magnitude_0 < v862 then
                                                v861 = v864;
                                                v862 = l_Magnitude_0;
                                            end;
                                        end;
                                    end;
                                end;
                            end;
                            if v861 then
                                if ViewKA then
                                    local l_HumanoidRootPart_1 = v861.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
                                    if l_HumanoidRootPart_1 then
                                        local v877 = Instance.new("BillboardGui", l_HumanoidRootPart_1);
                                        v877.Adornee = l_HumanoidRootPart_1;
                                        v877.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 40);
                                        v877.AlwaysOnTop = true;
                                        local v878 = Instance.new("TextLabel", v877);
                                        v878.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0);
                                        v878.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
                                        v878.Text = traducao.Atacando;
                                        v878.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 0, 0);
                                        v878.TextStrokeTransparency = 0;
                                        v878.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold;
                                        v878.TextScaled = true;
                                        do
                                            local l_v877_0 = v877;
                                            task.delay(0.7, function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                                                -- upvalues: l_v877_0 (ref)
                                                l_v877_0:Destroy();
                                            end);
                                        end;
                                    end;
                                end;
                                AttackCH(v861);
                            end;
                            return;
                        end;
                    end);
                    return;
                end;
            end;

                        local l_Character_47 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character;
                        if not l_Character_47 then
                            return;
                        else
                            local l_HumanoidRootPart_10 = l_Character_47:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
                            local l_Humanoid_22 = l_Character_47:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
                            if not l_HumanoidRootPart_10 or not l_Humanoid_22 then
                                return;
                            else
                                VoidBlock = true;
                                if not AntiVoid then
                                    workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0;
                                end;
                                task.wait(0.1);
                                l_HumanoidRootPart_10.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999999999999, -999999999999999, 999999999999999);
                                l_Humanoid_22.Health = 0;
                                if not AntiVoid then
                                    task.wait(0.1);
                                    workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = -500;
                                end;
                                task.wait(2);
                                VoidBlock = false;
                                return;
                            end;
                        end;
                    end)();
                    return;
                end;
            end;

                if VoidBlock then
                    return;

                    coroutine.wrap(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                        local l_LocalPlayer_28 = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
                        local l_Character_48 = l_LocalPlayer_28.Character;
                        if not l_Character_48 then
                            return;
                        else
                            local l_HumanoidRootPart_11 = l_Character_48:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");

                                return;

                                VoidBlock = true;

                                while true do
                                    if l_Humanoid_23.FloorMaterial ~= Enum.Material.Air or tick() - v1609 > 3 then
                                        workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = -2000;
                                        workspace.Gravity = math.huge;
                                        task.wait(0.1);
                                        l_HumanoidRootPart_11.Position = Vector3.new(l_HumanoidRootPart_11.Position.X, workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight, l_HumanoidRootPart_11.Position.Z);
                                        l_HumanoidRootPart_11.Parent = workspace;
                                        task.wait(0.1);
                                        workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = -500;
                                        workspace.Gravity = 196.1999969482422;
                                        task.wait(0.1);
                                        if AntiVoid then
                                            workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0;

                                        task.delay(2, function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]

                                        VoidBlock = false;
                                        return;
                                    else
                                        task.wait(0.1);
                                    end;
                                end;
                            end;
                        end;
                    end)();
                    return;
                end;

            GlobalKillChat = function(v1623, v1624) --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                if not ativo then
                    return;
                elseif OnlySL and not table.find(Safelist, v1623) then
                    return;
                elseif AtacandoGlobal then
                    return;
                else
                    v1624 = v1624:lower();
                    if v1624:sub(1, 5) ~= ":kill" then
                        return;
                    else
                        local v1625 = v1624:sub(7):lower();
                        if v1625 == "" then
                            return;
                        else
                            local l_Players_9 = game:GetService("Players");
                            local v1627 = nil;
                            for _, v1629 in pairs(l_Players_9:GetPlayers()) do
                                if v1629 ~= l_Players_9.LocalPlayer then
                                    local v1630 = v1629.Name:lower();
                                    local v1631 = v1629.DisplayName:lower();
                                    if (v1630:sub(1, #v1625) == v1625 or v1631:sub(1, #v1625) == v1625) and Protegido(v1629.Name) then
                                        if v1629.Name == v1623 or v1629 == l_Players_9.LocalPlayer.Name then
                                            Say("Attacking yourself or me is not allowed!");
                                            return;
                                        else
                                            local l_Character_49 = v1629.Character;
                                            local v1633 = l_Character_49 and l_Character_49:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
                                            local v1634 = l_Character_49 and l_Character_49:FindFirstChildOfClass("ForceField");
                                            local v1635 = l_Character_49 and l_Character_49:FindFirstChild("Kawaii Revolver") or v1629:FindFirstChild("Backpack") and v1629.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Kawaii Revolver");
                                            if v1633 and v1633.Health > 0 and not v1634 and v1635 then
                                                v1627 = v1629;
                                                local l_Character_50 = l_Players_9.LocalPlayer.Character;
                                                if l_Character_50 and l_Character_50:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                                    posGK = l_Character_50.HumanoidRootPart.Position;
                                                    break;
                                                else
                                                    posGK = nil;
                                                    break;
                                                end;
                                            end;
                                        end;
                                    end;
                                end;
                            end;
                            if not v1627 then
                                Say(traducao.AlvoInText);
                                return;
                            else
                                DesligarBotao(LoopBotao);
                                DesligarBotao(FlingBotao);
                                DesligarBotao(CBringBotao);
                                local l_Character_51 = l_Players_9.LocalPlayer.Character;
                                if not l_Character_51 or not l_Character_51:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    return;
                                else
                                    local _ = l_Character_51.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
                                    AtacandoGlobal = true;
                                    LoopGlobalKillRenderStepped = game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function() --[[ Line: 0 ]] --[[ Name:  ]]
                                        -- upvalues: v1627 (ref), l_Character_51 (ref), l_Players_9 (ref)
                                        if not v1627 then
                                            return;
                                        else
                                            local l_Character_52 = v1627.Character;
                                            l_Character_51 = l_Players_9.LocalPlayer.Character;
                                            if not (l_Character_52 and l_Character_52:FindFirstChild("Head") and l_Character_52:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and l_Character_51 and l_Character_51:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
                                                AtacandoGlobal = false;
                                                v1627 = nil;
                                                if LoopGlobalKillRenderStepped then
                                                    LoopGlobalKillRenderStepped:Disconnect();
                                                    LoopGlobalKillRenderStepped = nil;
                                                end;
                                                Say(traducao.KilledText);
                                                if posGK and l_Character_51 and l_Character_51:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                                    l_Character_51.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(posGK);
                                                end;
                                                return;
                                            else
                                                local l_Humanoid_24 = l_Character_52.Humanoid;

                tempoDecorrido = 0;
                while true do
                    textoTempoLocal.Text = string.format("%s: %02d:%02d", traducao.GameTime, math.floor(tempoDecorrido / 60), tempoDecorrido % 60);
                    tempoDecorrido = tempoDecorrido + 1;
                    wait(1);
                end;
            end)();
